{"nick":"Sorella","message":"rickardo1: basically, Node *does* use more than one thread. It uses several. All of the expensive things get to run on all of those different threads. It's v8, the JS engine, that has only one thread. v8 runs *only* JS. But that JS can call functions that are implemented in C++. These functions implemented in C++ will start up a new thread and return","date":"2016-03-26T21:15:38.579Z","type":"message"}
